 Nowadays people are getting more attracted towards fish pedicure to maintain the health and beauty of the feet
 fish pedicor ek tarah kii therapy he
 In which the feet are put into a tub filled with fish
 tub main maujuud choti-choti machhliyaan aapke pairon se ded skin ko alag kar use kha jaati he
 Benefits of Fish Pedicure - The skin of the feet is softened by having a fish pedicure
 -fish pedicor karwaane se aapako pairon ke dard se nijaat milti he
 - Getting a fish pedicure is beneficial in diseases like eczema and psoriasis
 -fish pedicor karwaane ke liye aapako apni jeb par zyada jor bhi nahin daalana padegaa
 Let me tell, it is not too expensive
 -pedicor ke liye yuj kii jane vaali machhliyaan ded skin saaf karne ke saath sharir ke raktapravaah ko bhi badhaati he
 - The pedicure fishes named Gara rufa help to make the legs dead skin and make them beautiful and glowing
 fish pedicor ke nuksaan-aapane kai baar malls yaa parlor main logon ko ek hi tanks main apane pairon ko daalkar pedicor karavaate dekha hoga

 Fishes called Gara rufa are used to pedicure fish
 fish pedicor karavaate samay mahilaon ko in jaruri baton par jarur dhyaan dena chahie
 Otherwise it can affect your health
 aaie jaanate hai fish pedicor karavaate hue aakhir kin baton kaa dhyaan rakhana chahie
 - Many times people in the fish pedicure parlor and spa center do not change the tub water for several days
 isaki vajah se tanks main upasthit microbacteria ke kaaran aapako kai tarah kaa skin infections ho saktaa he
 While making a fish pedicure, keep in mind that the water of the tub is changed daily and the water is clean

 is pariksha main paas hone ke baad parikshaarthi piechdi karne ke saath-saath puure bharat main kisi bhi uniwarsity main shikshak banane ke yogya ho jate hai

 Some tips for preparing for UGC NET exam: 1
 pichley kuch saalon ke prashn-patron ko jarur dekh len
 This helps in understanding the exam pattern and important topics
 isse aapkaa aatm-vishwaas to badhata hi he, saath hi aapaki taiyaari bhi sahi disha main chalati he
 The help of your seniors and teachers should also be sought if needed
 2
 You should be fully familiar with your syllabus
 ab saare prashn objective hi aate hai, isliye kisi bhi topic ko chhodana nahin chahie
 3
 aapako kuch vishyon ko praathamikta deni chahie
 This exam covers most of the topics of your PG course so you should have a strong grip on every subject
 general awarenes ke test peparon ko jarur hal karnaa chahie
 4
 personal nots jarur banane chahie
 These notes are very useful for 'last-minute study'
 5
 Large note-books or registers should be kept
 note book ko teen kollam main baant le
 Write the topic, title, serial number in the left column, the main cut in the middle column and any updates or references in the last column
 6
 You should do your preparation properly
 aapako yah pataa hona chahie ki koun sa vishay kitna or kitni der ke liye padhanaa he
 Should not be a waste of time
 7
 The most important thing is that you should be positive and full of self-confidence
 aatm-vishwaas se aapaki taiyaari kaa pataa chalata he

 (input bhashaa se) Delhi residents may have to worry about traffic problems for the next 20 days due to a big pit on Bhairon Mandir Road in Delhi
 ringrod se bhairon road par aate hi siver kii pipe line main licage kii vajah se is gadde kii shuruyaat ravivaar ko hui thi lekin use somvaar ko thik kar liya gaya tha
 But on Tuesday, this pit became very large and leakage is continuously happening in the pipeline, due to which the PWD cannot work on building the road until the leakage is rectified
 tippaniyan Although the Minister of Delhi Government had said that work is being done on a war footing, but according to Jal Board officials, work is being done to first close the sewer pipeline on both sides and drain the water pump
 line band karne ke baad licage thik kiya jaayegaa or licage thik hone ke baad hi dhansi hui sadak ko thik kiya ja sakegaa
 This entire process may take about 20 days
 jal board ke adhikariyon ke mutabik sadak dhansane se 28 foot gaharaa gadhdha ho gaya he
 The depth of the sewer line is about 40 feet
 siver line tak pahuchane ke baad hi saafe hoga kii licage kitna bada he
 According to officials, this sewer line was built in 1956, which has become dilapidated at many places
 trephic police kaa kahana he do jagahon par trephic ko divert kiya gaya he jisaki vajah se ringrod, itio, pragati maidan or south dilli main moolchand, ashram chowk par kaaphi jam ho saktaa he

 Congress legislator Deepak Saxena, who was elected from Chhindwara in the assembly elections held two months ago, resigned from the membership of the assembly on Wednesday
 ajtak se phone par baat karte hue deepak saxena ne istife kii pushti kii he
 Although his resignation was accepted or not, it has not yet been confirmed by the Speaker
 kaha ja rahaa he ki unhone chhindwara seat mukhyamantri kamalnath ke liye khaali kii he taaki mukhyamantri chhindwara vidhansabha seat se upachunaav lard saken
 Chief Minister Kamal Nath is not an MLA at the moment and within six months of taking oath of Chief Minister, he is required to become an MLA and in such a situation since his becoming CM, there were questions about where he will contest the assembly elections
 kamalnath agar vidhayak chun liye gaye to phir unhen sansad kii sadsyta se bhi istipha dena hoga
 Chhindwara is considered one of the safest seats in the Congress where both Lok Sabha and Assembly seats are held by the Congress

 Rajiv Gandhi Khel Ratna Awards were given to the best players from 1992 to 2001, there was hardly any noise because Vishwanathan Anand, Leander Paes, Sachin Tendulkar, Dhanraj Pillai and Pullela Gopichand did so much before winning these awards
 It was not right for anyone to point fingers at them
 saal 200102 ke liye shooter abhinav bindra ko jab yah khitaab mila us vakt vah sirf 20 saal ke the, haalanki usase pehle unhone karname to kiye the, lekin aalochak un par sawaal uthaane se nahin chuke

 khitaab kaa sahi hakdaar sabit kar diya

 jab desh main dharmasthalon par bajte laudspikar ko lekar bavaal machaa he tab mumbai main ek aisi muslim shakhsiyat saamne ai he jisane musalmaan hokar bhi laudspikar par chalati ajaan kaa khulkar or lagaataar virodh kiya he
 Mohammed Ali alias Babubhai of Mumbai is a 66-year-old Namaji Muslim and considers azaan given by loudspeakers as un-islamic
 apni baat ko manwaane ke liye dhalati umr main unhone hoicourt main pitishan lagaai

 NDTV se exlusive baatcheet main yachikakarta mohammad ali urf babubhai ne kaha ki laudspikar kaa istemaal dharm kaa hissaa nahin he
 Nor is it basic
 kyonki dharm 1400 saal purana he or laudspikar abhi kuch sau saal pehle aayaa he
 Removing loudspeakers is not a threat to religion
 dharm apane aap main mukammal he
 He is not lame to make him powerful by giving him a loudspeaker crutch
 babu bhai kii kanoonee jeet ab ek muhim main tabdeel ho gai he
 To strengthen his claim, he has also found 64 edicts of clerics with scripture
 ve lagataar bataate hai ki unki ladaai dharm ke khilaaf nahin balki dharm ke naam par rosemara ke aacharan main jodi gai atirikt or gairajaruri baton ke khilaaf he
 Quoting the Quran, he has removed all the horns from seven mosques in Muslim-dominated areas like Behram Pada and Bharat Nagar in Mumbai
 unki ladaai main saath dene waalon ko himmat jutaney main bhi vakt laga
 Mohammad Nazar, a trustee of the local Madni mosque, told NDTV India that there were three speakers in his mosque
 inhen ek saath nahin balki dhire-dhire hataaya
 Removed it first in Azan, then in Namaz and in Jumme
 tippaniyan Hearing together the petitions of Santosh Pachalag, Dr
 Bedekar and Mohammad Ali three, regarding the loudspeakers ringing at the shrines, Justice Oak and Justice Syed Amjad of the Bombay High Court ruled in August 2016 that loudspeakers can be used anywhere in the country at night
 Those doing between 6 am to 6 am will be fined up to Rs 1 lakh and imprisoned for up to five years
 gauratlab he ki babubhai ne apni baat rakhane ke liye soshal media par bolne ke bajaae sanvaidhanik haq kaa istemaal kiya
